***фильм.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:фильм.html>фильм</a> (1259)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">film</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фильм.html>фильм</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">filʹm</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фильм.html>фи́льма</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фильм.html>фи́льмы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фильм.html>фи́льмов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>film, movie
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">короткометра́жный <b><a href = vnd.unilang:фильм.html>фильм</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">korotkometrážnyj <b>filʹm</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">short film</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><b>фильт<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ро<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ва́ть</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:финансировать.html>финанси́ровать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">finansírovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ание</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-anije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:финансирование.html>финанси́рование</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">finansírovanije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:финансирование.html>финанси́рования</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:финансирование.html>финанси́рования</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:финансирование.html>финанси́рований</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:финансировать.html>финанси́ровать</a> (13523)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">finanzieren</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">financer</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:финансировать.html>финанси́ровать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">finansírovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr> or <abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:финансировать.html>финанси́ровать</a></strong></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">профинанси́ровать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to finance, to fund</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. </p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:прилагательное.html>Прилага́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:относительный.html>относи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:финансы.html>финансы</a> (6472)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:финансы.html>фина́нсы</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">finánsy</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> <abbr title="plural number">pl</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:финансы.html>фина́нсов</a></b>, <i>plural only</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>finance <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">management of money and other assets, the monetary resources</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***финишировать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:финишировать.html>финиши́ровать</a> (30636)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:финиш.html>фи́ниш</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">fíniš</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ровать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-írovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:финишировать.html>финиши́ровать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">finišírovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr> or <abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to finish, to come in</li></ol>

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:женский.html>же́нский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 1-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 1a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. </p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-фирм-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:фирменный.html>фи́рменный</a> (8795)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фирма.html>фи́рма</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">fírma</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-енный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ennyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фирменный.html>фи́рменный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">fírmennyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)фи́рменнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)фи́рменней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> firm, company, brand; proprietary
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:фирменный.html>фи́рменное</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:блюдо.html>блю́до</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>fírmennoje</b> bljúdo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">house specialty</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally"><b>proprietary</b> dish</span>”)</div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:фирменный.html>фи́рменный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:знак.html>знак</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>fírmennyj</b> znak</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>proprietary</b> mark, trademark</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:фирменный.html>фи́рменный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:счет.html>счёт</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>fírmennyj</b> sčót</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>company</b> account</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:фирменный.html>фи́рменное</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:наименование.html>наименова́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>fírmennoje</b> naimenovánije</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>brand</b> name</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:фирменный.html>фи́рменный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:стиль.html>стиль</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>fírmennyj</b> stilʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>corporate</b> style</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> very good, high-quality</li></ol>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">fiche</i>  + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фишка.html>фи́шка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">fíška</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рыжий.html>фи́шки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рыжий.html>фи́шки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фишка.html>фи́шек</a></b>)

***флаг.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:флаг.html>флаг</a> (3638)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">vlag</i>. Influenced by English <i>flag</i> (as by spelling with ф instead of <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a>) so as not to clash with влах, "Vlach".
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:флаг.html>флаг</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">flag</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:флаг.html>фла́га</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:флаг.html>фла́ги</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:флаг.html>фла́гов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>flag, banner</li></ol>

***флагман.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:флагман.html>флагман</a> (9258)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:флагман.html>фла́гман</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">flágman</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:флагман.html>фла́гмана</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:флагман.html>фла́гманы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:флагман.html>фла́гманов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>admiral, flagship <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">the ship which carries the admiral, the flagship</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
